6RwAWZtK5UwdelimeterByIshitaThe reason, I believe, why this film is so underrated (especially by audiences) is the fact that, much like Kubrick&#39;s &quot;Barry Lyndon,&quot; it leans toward a more meditative style, reflecting and analyzing the psyche of its two lead characters rather than engaging in the typical gratuitous standoff/shootout sequences with rapid-fire editing, while also presenting its characters not as mythical figures (a common clichÃ© of the Western genre), but as simple, ordinary, flawed men who are not actually tough but just happen to be prone to violence and greed. Also, it&#39;s quite more leisurely paced than &quot;There Will Be Blood&quot; (an equally great picture) and less action-centered than &quot;<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6RwAWZtK5Uw&amp;t=3m10s">3:10</a> to Yuma&quot; (a considerably inferior picture). In a nutshell, it&#39;s a masterpiece.
